<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item
2.02.&nbsp; Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</font></b></h4>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information in this Current Report is being
furnished and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the purposes of Section&nbsp;18
of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the
liabilities of that Section.&nbsp; The information in this Current Report shall
not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other
document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 18, 2007, Kraft Foods Inc. issued an earnings
release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended March 31,
2007.&nbsp; A copy of the earnings release is attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></h1>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kraft
Foods Reports Progress on Growth Strategy</font></u></b></h1>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 42.5pt;text-indent:-12.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>First
quarter net revenues increased 5.7% to $8.6 billion; organic net revenues(1)
grew 3.6%.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 42.5pt;text-indent:-12.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>First
quarter diluted EPS decreased 29.5% to $0.43; diluted EPS excluding items that
affect comparability(2) decreased 2.2% to $0.44.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 42.5pt;text-indent:-12.25pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>2007
guidance remains unchanged.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NORTHFIELD, Ill. &#151; April 18, 2007 &#151; Kraft Foods Inc.
(NYSE: KFT) today reported solid first quarter revenue growth as the company
began implementing its growth strategy.&#160;
Earnings excluding items affecting comparability declined reflecting
investments in growth, including product quality, new business initiatives,
systems and distribution infrastructure.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The first quarter of
2007 was an eventful one for Kraft as we became independent from Altria and
began executing the strategic plan we announced in February,&#148; said Irene
Rosenfeld, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer.&#160; &#147;While our first quarter results reflect continued
improvement in several core categories, we still face many challenges. &#160;We expect to see further progress,
particularly in the second half of the year, as we set the stage for Kraft&#146;s
return to consistent growth.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">First quarter 2007 net
revenues increased 5.7% to $8.6 billion reflecting a favorable 1.2 percentage
point impact from the United Biscuits Iberia acquisition and a favorable 2.1
percentage point impact from currency. Divested businesses reduced net revenues
1.2 percentage points. Organic net revenues grew 3.6% reflecting volume growth
of 1.2 percentage points led by North America Snacks &amp; Cereals and
Convenient </font></p>

<div style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
company&#146;s top-line guidance measure is organic net revenues, which excludes the
impacts of acquisitions, divestitures and currency.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
company is presenting various operating results, such as operating income,
operating income margin, effective tax rate, net earnings and diluted EPS on
both a reported basis and on a basis excluding items that affect comparability
of results. The term &#147;items&#148; refers to asset impairment, exit and
implementation costs; gains and losses on the sales of businesses; interest
from tax reserve transfers from Altria Group, Inc.; and the favorable
resolution of Altria Group, Inc.&#146;s 1996-1999 IRS Tax Audit in 2006.&#160; Management believes these non-GAAP measures
are useful to investors because they provide an additional comparison of
year-to-year results.&#160; A reconciliation
of all non-GAAP measures to the nearest comparable GAAP used in this earnings
release can be found on the company&#146;s website, www.kraft.com.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\fc\10815110705_H11181_2016165\11584-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 18 15:11 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Meals, European Union and Developing Markets(3), as
well as favorable product mix of 2.2 percentage points from solid gains across
most businesses.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">First quarter 2007
diluted earnings per share were $0.43, down 29.5% from $0.61 in 2006.&#160; During first quarter 2007, the company
incurred $0.03 per diluted share ($88 million before taxes) in asset
impairment, exit and implementation costs against its cost restructuring
program, which was offset by the recognition of one-time interest income of
$0.03 per diluted share ($77 million before taxes) from tax reserve transfers
of $375 million from Altria Group, Inc. (NYSE: MO) primarily related to the
spin-off from Altria.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 60.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;"><!-- SET mrlHTMLTableCenter --><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Items&nbsp;Affecting&nbsp;Diluted&nbsp;EPS&nbsp;Comparability</font></u></p>

<div style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 60.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 60.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">* Does not add due to rounding.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">First quarter diluted
earnings per share excluding items declined 2.2% to $0.44 in 2007.&#160; Diluted earnings per share excluding items
reflect a $0.01 benefit from share repurchase activity offset by a $0.01
negative impact from </font>prior
year income from divested operations and a negative $0.01 impact from an
increase in the company&#146;s tax rate compared to 2006.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operating income
increased 10.3% from the prior year to $1.1 billion.&#160; Operating income excluding items declined
3.0% as the benefits of revenue growth were offset by a $35 million impact from
previously completed divestitures.&#160; First
quarter operating income margin excluding items decreased to 14.0% in 2007 from
15.2% in 2006 reflecting favorable product mix that was offset by higher
investments in marketing and quality improvements, investments in systems and
distribution infrastructure, higher input costs and </font>prior year divested operations.</p>

<div style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="left" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Developing Markets segment includes results of the Eastern Europe, Middle East
&amp; Africa (EEMA), Latin America and Asia Pacific regions.&#160; This segment was formerly called Developing
Markets, Oceania &amp; North Asia.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\10815110705_H11181_2016165\11584-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 18 15:11 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company&#146;s tax
rate in first quarter 2007 was 33.6%.&#160;
The company&#146;s effective tax rate excluding items was 32.3% in first
quarter 2007 compared to an effective tax rate of 30.8% in first quarter 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first quarter, the company
repurchased 5.9 million of its shares at a total cost of $187 million.&#160; A new $5.0 billion share repurchase plan went
into effect immediately following the company&#146;s spin-off from Altria Group,
Inc.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Discussion
of Results by Segment</font></u></b></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" bgcolor="white" style="background:white;border-collapse:collapse;font-family:Times New Roman;width:100.0%;">
 <tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
  <td width="41%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:41.56%;">
  <p style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;line-height:8.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><!-- SET mrlHTMLTableFull --></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:3.12%;">
  <p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:8.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="51%" colspan="7" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:51.48%;">
  <p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:8.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;">First&nbsp;Quarter<br>
  (%&nbsp;growth)</font></b></p>

  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0pt .7pt 0pt 0pt;width:3.82%;">

<p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">North America Beverages</font></u></i></b> organic net revenues grew 3.9% primarily
driven by favorable product mix in powdered beverages and coffee.&#160; The
introduction of <i>Crystal Light</i> with antioxidants and functional benefits as
well as the continued success of single-serve sticks led to strong powdered beverage growth.&#160; Coffee benefited from continued strong
performance in premium brands including <i>Starbucks</i>,
<i>Gevalia</i> and <i>Tassimo</i> partially offset by volume
declines in mainstream coffee.&#160;
Operating income excluding items declined 5.3% as revenue growth from
favorable product mix was offset by incremental investments behind new products
and higher green coffee costs.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">North America Cheese &amp; Foodservice</font></u></i></b> organic net revenues grew 0.5% reflecting
solid cheese volume gains and Foodservice price increases that were partially
offset by lower Foodservice volume from the discontinuation of lower margin
product lines.&#160; Cheese gains were driven
by growth in cream cheese, including the introduction of <i>Philadelphia</i> Ready-to-Eat Cheesecake,
gains in snacking cheese as </p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\fc\10815110705_H11181_2016165\11584-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 18 15:11 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">well as topping cheese from the introduction of <i>Grate It Fresh</i>.&#160; Operating income excluding items declined
2.8% as the contribution from organic revenue growth was offset by higher
marketing support.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">North America Convenient Meals</font></u></i></b> organic net revenues grew 4.8% from a
combination of favorable product mix from new product introductions, higher
volume driven by quality improvements and market share gains in the deli meats
and macaroni and cheese categories.&#160; New
product gains reflected the ongoing
success of <i>Kraft Easy-Mac </i>cups
and new varieties of <i>California Pizza
Kitchen</i> pizzas, the
introduction of <i>Oscar Mayer Deli Creations</i> sandwiches and the recent launch of <i>DiGiorno </i>Ultimate pizza.&#160;
Strong volume gains were driven by recent quality investments in <i>Kraft</i> macaroni and cheese and <i>DiGiorno</i> and <i>Tombstone</i> pizzas.&#160; Operating
income excluding items declined 9.2% as gains from organic revenue growth were
offset by investments in quality, manufacturing capacity and marketing support
as well as $12 million in prior year income from divested operations.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">North America </font></u></i></b><b><i><u style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Grocery</u></i></b> organic net revenues were flat compared to
prior year.&#160; Growth and market share
gains in better-for-you snacks such as <i>Jell-O</i>
sugar-free ready-to-eat pudding and sugar-free <i>Cool
Whip</i> topping were offset by category weakness and share declines in <i>Kraft</i> salad dressings.&#160; Operating income excluding items declined
2.8% due to unfavorable product mix and lower volume.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">North America </font></u></i></b><b><i><u style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Snacks
&amp; Cereals</u></i></b>
organic net revenues grew 4.1% behind solid volume and mix gains primarily in
cookies and crackers.&#160; Cookie growth
reflected new product successes in the<i> Chips Ahoy! </i>and
<i>Newtons </i>franchises that were partially
offset by lower <i>Oreo</i> volume due
to a recent price increase.&#160; Strong
cracker growth was driven by new products in <i>Wheat
Thins</i> and <i>Triscuit</i>.&#160; Operating income excluding items declined
2.0% as gains from organic revenue growth and lower manufacturing costs were
offset by $24 million in prior year income from divested operations as well as
investments in quality and growth initiatives.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">European Union</font></u></i></b> organic net revenues grew 2.9% reflecting
strong chocolate revenues across most markets behind new <i>Milka</i> and <i>Freia
Marabou</i> products as well as growth in premium offerings such as <i>Cote d&#146;Or</i>.&#160;
In coffee, increased promotional spending to counter price-based
competition in mainstream roast and ground coffee offset growth in <i>Tassimo</i>.&#160;
The addition of the United Biscuits businesses contributed 6.6
percentage points to reported net revenue growth and favorable currency added
9.8 percentage points.&#160; Operating income
excluding items increased 3.3% as revenue growth was partially offset by higher
promotional and marketing expenses as well as higher green coffee costs.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\fc\10815110705_H11181_2016165\11584-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 18 15:11 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Developing Markets</font></u></i></b> organic net revenues grew 8.9% led by double-digit growth in Eastern
Europe, Middle East &amp; Africa (EEMA) and Latin America.&#160;
Gains in EEMA were driven by <i>Jacobs</i> and <i>Carte Noire</i> soluble coffee.&#160; In Latin America, strong revenue growth was
driven by new products and increased marketing support in all three core
categories: chocolate, biscuits and powdered beverages.&#160; These gains were partially offset by lower
revenue in Asia Pacific due to volume declines in Australia, primarily in
cheese.&#160; Operating income excluding
items was up 13.6% as the contribution
from strong revenue growth was partially offset by incremental investments in
marketing and distribution as well as higher input costs.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2007
Outlook</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 3.0pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company confirmed its guidance for 2007.&#160; The company expects organic net revenue
growth of 3%-4% for the full year and fully diluted EPS in the range of $1.50
to $1.55, or $1.75 to $1.80 excluding items.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reflected in this
guidance, the company expects to incur costs of approximately $625 million in
2007, or $0.25 per fully diluted share, under its previously announced cost
restructuring program.&#160; Additionally, the
company continues to expect cumulative savings from the program to reach
approximately $700 million by year-end.&#160;
To date, cumulative savings from this cost restructuring program on an
annualized basis to date totaled approximately $615 million, up from
approximately $540 million at the end of 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also reflected in
its guidance, the company continues to expect its 2007 full-year effective tax
rate excluding items to average 35.5%.&#160;
The company&#146;s effective tax rate was 32.3% in first quarter 2007
reflecting the benefit of consolidation with Altria Group, Inc. during the
quarter.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; *&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;
*</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft Foods will host a
conference call for investors to review its results at 5 p.m. ET on April 18,
2007.&#160; Access to a live audio webcast is
available at www.kraft.com and a replay of the conference call will be
available on the company&#146;s web site.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft Foods (NYSE: KFT)
is one of the world&#146;s largest food and beverage companies with annual revenues
of more than $34 billion.&#160; For over 100
years, Kraft has offered consumers delicious and wholesome foods that fit the
way they live. Kraft markets a broad portfolio of iconic brands in 155
countries, including seven brands with revenue of more than $1 billion, such as
Kraft cheeses, dinners and dressings; Oscar Mayer meats; Philadelphia cream
cheese; Post cereals; Nabisco cookies and crackers; </font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\fc\10815110705_H11181_2016165\11584-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Apr 18 15:11 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Jacobs coffees and Milka chocolates.&#160; Kraft became a fully independent company on
March 30, 2007, and is listed in the Standard &amp; Poor&#146;s 100 and 500
indexes.&#160; The company also is a member of
the Dow Jones Sustainability Index and the Ethibel Sustainability Index.&#160; For more information, visit the company&#146;s
website at www.kraft.com.</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></u></b></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
press release contains projections of future results and other forward-looking
statements.&#160; One can identify these
forward-looking statements by use of words such as &#147;strategy,&#148; &#147;expects,&#148;
&#147;plans,&#148; &#147;anticipates,&#148; &#147;believes,&#148; &#147;will,&#148; &#147;continues,&#148; &#147;estimates,&#148;
&#147;intends,&#148; &#147;projects,&#148; &#147;goals,&#148; &#147;targets&#148; and other words of similar
meaning.&#160; One can also identify them by
the fact that they do not relate strictly to historical or current facts. These
statements are based on the company&#146;s current assumptions and estimates and are
subject to risks and uncertainties. In connection with the &#147;safe harbor&#148;
provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, the company
is hereby identifying important factors that could cause actual results and
outcomes to differ materially from those contained in any forward looking
statement made by or on behalf of the company.&#160;
These factors include: (a) the effect on the company of competition in
its markets, changes in consumer preferences and demand for its products,
including diet trends, changing prices for its raw materials and local economic
and market conditions; (b) the company&#146;s continued ability to promote brand
equity successfully, to anticipate and respond to new consumer trends, to
develop new products and markets, to broaden brand portfolios, to compete
effectively with lower priced products in a consolidating environment at the
retail and manufacturing levels and to improve productivity; (c) the company&#146;s
ability to consummate and successfully integrate acquisitions and to realize
the cost savings and improved asset utilization contemplated by its
restructuring program; (d) the impact of gains or losses, or lost operating
income, from the sales of businesses that are less of a strategic fit within
the company&#146;s portfolio; (e) the effects of foreign economies, changes in tax
requirements and currency movements; (f) fluctuations in levels of customer
inventories and credit and other business risks related to the operations of
the company&#146;s customers; (g) the company&#146;s access to credit markets, borrowing
costs and credit ratings; (h) the company&#146;s benefit expense, which is subject
to the investment performance of pension plan assets, interest rates and cost
increases for medical benefits offered to employees and retirees; (i) the
impact of recalls if products become adulterated or misbranded, liability if
product consumption causes injury, ingredient disclosure and labeling laws and
regulations, potential claims relating to false or deceptive advertising under
consumer protection or other laws and the possibility that consumers could lose
confidence in the safety and quality of certain food products; and (j) consumer
concerns regarding genetically modified organisms and the health implications
of obesity and trans fatty acids.&#160;
Developments in any of these areas could cause the company's results to
differ materially from results that have been or may be projected by or on
behalf of the company. The company cautions that the foregoing list of
important factors is not exclusive. For additional information on these and
other factors that could affect the company&#146;s forward-looking statements, see
the company&#146;s filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission, including
the company&#146;s most recently filed Annual Report on Form 10-K and subsequent
reports on Form 10-Q and 8-K. Any forward looking statements in this press
release are made as of the date hereof. The company does not undertake to
update any forward looking statement.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></u></b></h3>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">The company reports its
financial results in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles
(GAAP).&#160; Management believes that certain
non-GAAP measures and corresponding ratios provide additional meaningful
comparisons between current results and results in prior operating
periods.&#160; More specifically, management
believes these non-GAAP measures reflect fundamental business performance
because they exclude certain items that affect comparability of results.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">The company uses organic net
revenues and corresponding growth ratios as non-GAAP measures.&#160; Organic net revenues is defined as net
revenues excluding the impacts of acquisitions, divestitures and currency.&#160; Management believes this measure better
reflects revenues on a go-forward basis and provides improved comparability of
results.&#160; The company also uses non-GAAP
measures when presenting operating results, such as operating income; operating
income margin; effective tax rate; net earnings and diluted earnings per share;
as excluding items.&#160; The term &#147;items&#148;
refers to asset impairment, exit and implementation costs primarily related to
a restructuring program that began in the first quarter of 2004 (the &#147;Restructuring
Program&#148;).&#160; These restructuring charges
include separation-related costs, asset write-downs, and other costs related to
the implementation of the Restructuring Program.&#160; Other excluded items pertain to asset
impairment charges on certain long-lived assets; gains and losses on the sales
of businesses; </font>interest from tax reserve transfers from </font><font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Altria Group, Inc.; and
the favorable resolution of Altria Group, Inc.&#146;s 1996-1999 IRS Tax Audit in
2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">See the attached schedules for
supplemental financial data and corresponding reconciliations to GAAP financial
measures for the quarter ended March 31, 2007, and March 31, 2006.&#160; Non-GAAP financial measures should be viewed
in addition to, and not as an alternative for, the company&#146;s results prepared
in accordance with GAAP.&#160; In addition,
the non-GAAP measures the company is using may differ from non-GAAP measures
that other companies use.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 20.0pt;text-indent:-20.0pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Developing Markets segment includes results of the Eastern Europe, Middle East
and Africa (EEMA), Latin America and Asia Pacific regions. This segment was
formerly called Developing Markets, Oceania &amp; North Asia (DMONA).</p>
